(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

-= Welcome to TextWorld, ALFRED! =-. You are in the middle of a room. This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

            1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.

            3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
            4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

        In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

            Then, apply the object in a purposeful way — not just move it — but interact with the environment to fulfill the task’s actual goal.

            Hint: 
            1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.
            2. If you want to slice an object, you should first go to the receptacle where both the sharp object and the aim object are located and ONLY pick up the sharp object then do the slice action. Don't forget to put the sharp object back to the receptacle after you finish slicing.
            3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
            4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

        In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.
        
        Note: 
        1. some receptacles have numbers in their names. Always keep them as they are. For example, "towelholder1" should not be changed to "towelholder".
        2. Your initial goal should always be to go to a new location instead of put something into somewhere.
        3. Do not enter stage 2 when not finishing stage 1.

        Note: Always include :negative-preconditions in your :requirements whenever you use (not …) or delete effects, and never leave an :precondition or :effect block empty—either omit it or include at least one literal.

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

            3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
            4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

        In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )

    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?o ?r) (handfree))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)

    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )

    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )

    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )

    :effect (heated ?o)
  )

  (:types
    receptacle object - thing

    sharpObject - object
  )

    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )

  )

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )

    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)

    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))

  )

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
    (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
    (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
    (isFridge ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    sharpobject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (handfree)
    (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
    (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
    (isFridge ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpobject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    sharpobject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handfree)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
    (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
    (isFridge ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpobject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    sharpobject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handfree)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
    (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
    (isFridge ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpobject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)

(define (domain exploration-domain)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions :adl)
  (:types
    receptacle object - thing
    sharpObject - object
  )
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (closed ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (on ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (handfree)
    (sliced ?o - object)
    (heated ?o - object)
    (cleaned ?o - object)
    (cooled ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
    (isMicrowave ?r - receptacle)
    (isSinkbasin ?r - receptacle)
    (isFridge ?r - receptacle)
  )
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )
  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (closed ?r))
    :effect (and (not (closed ?r)) (opened ?r))
  )
  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (and (not (opened ?r)) (closed ?r))
  )
  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (handfree) (or (in ?o ?r) (on ?o ?r)))
    :effect (and (holding ?o) (not (in ?o ?r)) (not (on ?o ?r)) (not (handfree)))
  )
  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (on ?o ?r) (handfree))
  )
  (:action useObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (used ?o)
  )
  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isMicrowave ?r))
    :effect (heated ?o)
  )
  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isSinkbasin ?r))
    :effect (cleaned ?o)
  )
  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holding ?o) (at ?r) (isFridge ?r))
    :effect (cooled ?o)
  )
  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (in ?co ?r) (holding ?sharp_o))
    :effect (and (sliced ?co) (not (holding ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
  )
)
